MPT Beta','Active Share','Port. Ending Active Share']},\n  {id:'size',label:'Size & Concentration',color:'#38bdf8',keys:['Market Capitalization','# of Securities','Weighted Median Market Cap','Wt Avg Market Cap']},\n  {id:'valuation',label:'Valuation',color:'#fb923c',keys:['Price/Earnings','P/E','Price/Book','P/B','Price/Sales','P/S','Price/Cash Flow','Dividend Yield','Earnings Yield','EV/EBITDA']},\n  {id:'growth',label:'Growth',color:'#6366f1',keys:['EPS Growth','Earnings Growth','Revenue Growth','Sales Growth','Est. Margin','Net Margin','Operating Margin','Profit Margin','Debt/Equity','Current Ratio']}\n];\n\nfunction _chrGroup(metricName){\n  let mn=metricName.toLowerCase();\n  for(let g of CHR_GROUPS){\n    for(let k of g.keys){\n      if(mn.includes(k.toLowerCase()))return g;\n    }\n  }\n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction _chrProfile(chars){\n  // Derive a one-line portfolio profile from characteristics\n  let tags=[];\n  let find=(keywords)=>chars.find(c=>{let ml=c.m.toLowerCase();return keywords.some(k=>ml.includes(k));});\n  // Size tilt\n  let mc=find(['market cap','capitalization']);\n  if(mc&&mc.b!=null){\n    let pctDiff=mc.b!==0?(mc.p-mc.b)/Math.abs(mc.b)*100:0;\n    if(pctDiff<-15)tags.push({text:'Small-Cap Bias',cls:'tilt-size'});\n    else if(pctDiff>15)tags.push({text:'Large-Cap Tilt',cls:'tilt-size'});\n  }\n  // Valuation: P/E\n  let pe=find(['price/earnings','p/e']);\n  if(pe&&pe.b!=null){\n    let diff=pe.p-pe.b;\n    if(diff>2)tags.push({text:'Growth-Priced',cls:'tilt-growth'});\n    else if(diff<-2)tags.push({text:'Value-Priced',cls:'tilt-value'});\n  }\n  // Quality: ROE / FCF\n  let roe=find(['roe','return on equity']);\n  let fcf=find(['fcf','free cash flow']);\n  if(roe&&roe.b!=null&&(roe.p-roe.b)>1)tags.push({text:'Quality Overweight',cls:'tilt-quality'});\n  else if(fcf&&fcf.b!=null&&(fcf.p-fcf.b)>0.5)tags.push({text:'Quality Overweight',cls:'tilt-quality'});\n  // Growth\n  let eps=find(['eps growth','earnings growth']);\n  if(eps&&eps.b!=null&&(eps.p-eps.b)>2)tags.push({text:'Growth-Tilted',cls:'tilt-growth'});\n  // Risk\n  let te=find(['tracking error']);\n  if(te&&te.p>8)tags.push({text:'High Active Risk',cls:'tilt-risk'});\n  else if(te&&te.p<3)tags.push({text:'Low Active Risk',cls:'tilt-neutral'});\n  // Active share\n  let as=find(['active share']);\n  if(as&&as.p>80)tags.push({text:'High Conviction',cls:'tilt-quality'});\n  // Concentration\n  let nsec=find(['# of securities']);\n  if(nsec&&nsec.b!=null&&(nsec.p/nsec.b)<0.3)tags.push({text:'Concentrated',cls:'tilt-risk'});\n  if(!tags.length)tags.push({text:'Benchmark-Like',cls:'tilt-neutral'});\n  return tags;\n}\n\nfunction rChr(chars){\n  if(!chars.length)return'<p style=\"color:var(--txt);font-size:12px\">No characteristic data</p>';\n\n  // Compute diffs and find top 3 by absolute deviation (percentage-normalized)\n  let enriched=chars.map(c=>{\n    let diff=c.b!=null?c.p-c.b:null;\n    let absPctDev=diff!=null&&c.b!==0?Math.abs(diff/Math.abs(c.b)*100):diff!=null?Math.abs(diff):0;\n    let group=_chrGroup(c.m);\n    return{...c,diff,absPctDev,group};\n  });\n\n  // Sort by absolute deviation to find top 3\n  let ranked=[...enriched].filter(c=>c.diff!=null).sort((a,b)=>b.absPctDev-a.absPctDev);\n  let top3Set=new Set(ranked.slice(0,3).map(c=>c.m));\n\n  // Find max absolute diff for bar scaling\n  let maxAbsDiff=Math.max(...enriched.filter(c=>c.diff!=null).map(c=>Math.abs(c.diff)),1);\n\n  // Group metrics\n  let grouped=[];\n  let usedSet=new Set();\n  for(let g of CHR_GROUPS){\n    let members=enriched.filter(c=>c.group&&c.group.id===g.id);\n    if(members.length){\n      grouped.push({type:'header',group:g});\n      members.forEach(m=>{grouped.push({type:'row',data:m});usedSet.add(m.m);});\n    }\n  }\n  // Ungrouped metrics go under \"Other\"\n  let ungrouped=enriched.filter(c=>!usedSet.has(c.m));\n  if(ungrouped.length){\n    grouped.push({type:'header',group:{id:'other',label:'Other',color:'#94a3b8'}});\n    ungrouped.forEach(m=>grouped.push({type:'row',data:m}));\n  }\n\n  // Build profile summary\n  let profileTags=_chrProfile(chars);\n  let profileHtml=`<div class=\"chr-profile\"><span class=\"chr-icon\">&#9670;</span><div class=\"chr-tags\">${profileTags.map(t=>`<span class=\"chr-tag ${t.cls}\">${t.text}</span>`).join('')}</div></div>`;\n\n  // Build table rows\n  let rows=grouped.map(item=>{\n    if(item.type==='header'){\n      return`<tr class=\"chr-group-hdr\"><td colspan=\"4\"><span class=\"chr-grp-dot\" style=\"background:${item.group.color}\"></span>${item.group.label}</td></tr>`;\n    }\n    let c=item.data;\n    let diff=c.diff;\n    let cls=diff!=null&&diff>0?'pos':diff!=null&&diff<0?'neg':'';\n    let isTop3=top3Set.has(c.m);\n    let trCls='clickable'+(isTop3?' chr-top3':'');\n    // Deviation bar: centered bar expanding left (neg) or right (pos) from midpoint\n    let barHtml='';\n    if(diff!=null){\n      let pct=Math.min(Math.abs(diff)/maxAbsDiff*50,50);\n      let barCls=diff>=0?'pos-bar':'neg-bar';\n      let leftPos=diff>=0?'50%':(50-pct)+'%';\n      barHtml=`<div class=\"chr-bar-wrap\"><div class=\"chr-bar-track\"></div><div class=\"chr-bar-mid\"></div><div class=\"chr-bar-fill ${barCls}\" style=\"left:${leftPos};width:${pct}%\"></div></div>`;\n    }\n    let diffCell=diff!=null?`<div class=\"chr-devbar\"><span class=\"chr-val ${cls}\">${fp(diff,1)}</span>${barHtml}</div>`:'<span style=\"color:var(--txt)\">—</span>';\n    return`<tr class=\"${trCls}\" onclick=\"oDrChar('${c.m.replace(/'/g,\"\\\\'\")}')\"><td style=\"color:var(--txth)\">${c.m}${isTop3?'<span style=\"margin-left:4px;font-size:8px;color:var(--pri);font-weight:700\" title=\"Top deviation\">&#9679;</span>':''}</td><td class=\"r\" data-sv=\"${c.p}\">${f2(c.p,1)}</td><td class=\"r\" data-sv=\"${c.b??0}\">${f2(c.b,1)}</td><td class=\"r\" data-sv=\"${diff??0}\">${diffCell}</td></tr>`;\n  }).join('');\n\n  return profileHtml+`<table id=\"tbl-chr\"><thead><tr><th onclick=\"sortTbl('tbl-chr',0)\">Metric</th><th class=\"r\" onclick=\"sortTbl('tbl-chr',1)\">Portfolio</th><th class=\"r\" onclick=\"sortTbl('tbl-chr',2)\">Benchmark</th><th class=\"r\"
